## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Prometheus Metrics Exposition Pattern Across Kubernetes and Grafana

## Your Task

Find the Go source files in both kubernetes/kubernetes and grafana/grafana that implement the Prometheus metrics exposition pattern: where metrics are registered using the Prometheus client_golang library, how metric collectors are organized, and where the `/metrics` HTTP endpoint is configured to expose them. Compare how both projects structure their metrics infrastructure.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain. Both Kubernetes and Grafana use the Prometheus client_golang library to expose internal metrics, but they organize their metrics registration and exposition differently. Your goal is to map these patterns across both codebases.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/grafana--v11.4.0.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?
- **Symbol identification**: Correct symbol names and locations?
- **Keyword presence**: Did you mention key concepts (metrics registry, collectors, exposition)?

## Summary

### Kubernetes Metrics Infrastructure

**Registry**: Kubernetes builds a custom `KubeRegistry` abstraction (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go`) wrapping `prometheus.NewRegistry()`. The `kubeRegistry` struct adds version-aware metric lifecycle management (ALPHA/BETA/STABLE stability levels, automatic hiding of deprecated metrics based on the current k8s version). The global singleton lives in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go` as `defaultRegistry`.

**Collectors**: Custom collectors implement the `StableCollector` interface via `BaseStableCollector` (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/collector.go`), with `DescribeWithStability`/`CollectWithStability` methods. Standard metric types (Counter, Gauge, Histogram, Summary) are wrapped in lazy-init structs that implement `Registerable`.

**`/metrics` endpoint**: `DefaultMetrics.Install` in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go` mounts `legacyregistry.Handler()` → `promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...)` at `/metrics`. A separate `/metrics/slis` endpoint uses its own `KubeRegistry`.

### Grafana Metrics Infrastructure

**Registry**: Grafana uses a `multiRegistry` gatherer (`pkg/infra/metrics/service.go`) combining the k8s `legacyregistry.DefaultGatherer` (wrapped in `addPrefixWrapper` to ensure `grafana_` prefix) and `prometheus.DefaultGatherer`. The registerer is `legacyregistry.Registerer()` (reusing the k8s package).

**Metric definitions**: All metrics are defined as package-level `prometheus.*` variables in `pkg/infra/metrics/metrics.go` with namespace `ExporterName = "grafana"`, bulk-registered via `initMetricVars(reg)` in `Prov
... (truncated)

their metrics infrastructure quite differently.\\n\\n## Kubernetes Metrics Infrastructure\\n\\n### Registry Layer\\nKubernetes wraps the Prometheus registry in a custom abstraction called `KubeRegistry` (interface) and `kubeRegistry` (struct), defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go`. The `kubeRegistry` embeds a `PromRegistry` (itself an interface wrapping `prometheus.Registerer` + `prometheus.Gatherer`, defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/wrappers.go`) and adds Kubernetes-specific lifecycle management: version-aware metric hiding/deprecation, resettable metrics, and stability levels (ALPHA/BETA/STABLE).\\n\\nThe constructor `NewKubeRegistry()` calls `newKubeRegistry(BuildVersion())`, which creates a fresh `prometheus.NewRegistry()` and stores the Kubernetes binary version so that deprecated metrics can be automatically hidden based on the current version.\\n\\nThe global singleton is in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go`: `defaultRegistry = metrics.NewKubeRegistry()`. This package exposes package-level functions `MustRegister`, `RawMustRegister`, `Register`, `DefaultGatherer`, and `Registerer` that delegate to the global registry. On `init()`, it registers `collectors.NewProcessCollector` and `collectors.NewGoCollector` (standard Prometheus process/Go runtime collectors), then calls `RegisterMetaMetrics()` to track counts of registered/disabled/hidden metrics.\\n\\n### Metric Types\\nKubernetes wraps each Prometheus metric type (Counter, Gauge, Histogram, Summary) in its own struct (e.g., `Counter` in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/counter.go`) that implements the `Registerable` interface. These wrappers use lazy initialization: the underlying Prometheus metric is only created when `Create(*semver.Version)` is called during registration, at which point the metric's stability level and deprecation version are evaluated against the current Kubernetes version.\\n\\nFor custom collectors, Kubernetes provides the `StableCollector` interface and `BaseStableCollector` base struct in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/collector.go`. Custom collectors implement `DescribeWithStability` and `CollectWithStability` methods, and are registered via `CustomRegister`/`CustomMustRegister` on the `KubeRegistry`.\\n\\n### HTTP Exposition\\nThe `/metrics` HTTP endpoint is configured in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go`. The `DefaultMetrics` struct's `Install` method calls `legacyregistry.Handler()` and mounts it at `/metrics` on a `PathRecorderMux`. `legacyregistry.Handler()` returns `promhttp.InstrumentMetricHandler(prometheus.DefaultRegisterer, promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...))`. There is also `MetricsWithReset` which uses `legacyregistry.HandlerWithReset()` to support DELETE-triggered metric resets.\\n\\nThe underlying `HandlerFor` and `HandlerWithReset` functions are defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/http.go`, which delegate to `promhttp.HandlerFor`. Before mounting, the `register()` function in `routes/metrics.go` calls `Register()` on several subsystem metric packages (apiserver endpoints, etcd3, cacher, flowcontrol, peerproxy, handlers).\\n\\nFor SLI metrics, a separate registry (`Registry = metrics.NewKubeRegistry()`) is created in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/slis/registry.go`, and `SLIMetrics.Install` mounts it at `/metrics/slis` via `metrics.HandlerFor(Registry, ...)` in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/slis/routes.go`.\\n\\nComponent-specific metrics (e.g., kubelet in `pkg/kubelet/metrics/metrics.go`, kube-scheduler in `cmd/kube-scheduler/app/server.go`) register their metrics via `legacyregistry.MustRegister` in `init()` functions, following the standard Go init-based registration pattern.\\n\\n## Grafana Metrics Infrastructure\\n\\n### Registry Layer\\nGrafana uses the Prometheus `client_golang` library directly (not a custom wrapper) for metric definitions, but employs a multi-registry gatherer pattern. The registry and gatherer are provided via dependency injection (Wire) through `ProvideRegisterer()` and `ProvideGatherer()` in `pkg/infra/metrics/service.go`.\\n\\n`ProvideRegisterer()` returns `legacyregistry.Registerer()` \u2014 notably, Grafana reuses the Kubernetes `k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry` package as its registerer. `ProvideGatherer()` returns a `multiRegistry` that combines two gatherers: (1) an `addPrefixWrapper` around `legacyregistry.DefaultGatherer` (which prefixes all k8s-style metric names with `grafana_` unless they already start with `grafana_` or `go_`), and (2) `prometheus.DefaultGatherer` (the standard Prometheus default registry). This dual-gatherer approach merges metrics from both the k8s-style registry and the standard Prometheus default registry.\\n\\n### Metric Definitions\\nAll Grafana application metrics are defined as package-level variables in `pkg/infra/metrics/metrics.go` using standard `prometheus.NewCounter`, `prometheus.NewGaugeVec`, `prometheus.NewSummary`, `prometheus.NewHistogram`, etc. calls in an `init()` function. The namespace `ExporterName = \\\"grafana\\\"` is used for all metrics. The `initMetricVars(reg prometheus.Registerer)` function bulk-registers all metrics with the provided registerer via `reg.MustRegister(...)`.\\n\\nFrontend metrics (browser performance histograms) are defined and registered separately in `pkg/infra/metrics/frontendmetrics.go` via `initFrontendMetrics(reg)`, called from `ProvideService`. Helper utilities in `pkg/infra/metrics/metricutil/utils.go` provide `NewCounterStartingAtZero` and `NewCounterVecStartingAtZero` to pre-initialize counters at zero for all label combinations.\\n\\n`ProvideService` (the Wire-injected service constructor) calls `initMetricVars(reg)` and `initFrontendMetrics(reg)` to register all metrics, then reads configuration for optional Graphite bridge forwarding.\\n\\n### HTTP Exposition\\nThe `/metrics` HTTP endpoint is implemented as a middleware function `metricsEndpoint` in `pkg/api/http_server.go` (line 662). It is registered as a middleware via `m.Use(hs.metricsEndpoint)` in `addMiddlewaresAndStaticRoutes`. The handler checks `ctx.Req.URL.Path == \\\"/metrics\\\"` and, if enabled (`MetricsEndpointEnabled`), serves metrics using `promhttp.HandlerFor(hs.promGatherer, promhttp.HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true})`. The `promGatherer` is the `multiRegistry` provided by `ProvideGatherer()`. Optional basic auth is supported via `MetricsEndpointBasicAuthUsername`/`MetricsEndpointBasicAuthPassword` configuration.\\n\\n## Comparison\\n\\n| Aspect | Kubernetes | Grafana |\\n|---|---|---|\\n| Registry abstraction | Custom `KubeRegistry`/`kubeRegistry` wrapping `prometheus.Registry` | Direct `prometheus.Registerer` + custom `multiRegistry` gatherer |\\n| Global registry | `legacyregistry.defaultRegistry` (KubeRegistry) | `legacyregistry.Registerer()` (k8s registry) + `prometheus.DefaultGatherer` |\\n| Metric registration | `legacyregistry.MustRegister` in `init()` per package | `initMetricVars(reg)` bulk registration in `ProvideService` |\\n| Collector pattern | `StableCollector`/`BaseStableCollector` for custom collectors | Standard `prometheus.Collector` interface |\\n| `/metrics` endpoint | `DefaultMetrics.Install` \u2192 `legacyregistry.Handler()` \u2192 `promhttp.HandlerFor` | `metricsEndpoint` middleware \u2192 `promhttp.HandlerFor(promGatherer, ...)` |\\n| Stability/versioning | Built-in stability levels (ALPHA/BETA/STABLE) and version-based hiding | None (uses standard Prometheus) |\\n| Additional endpoints | `/metrics/slis` for SLI metrics via separate `KubeRegistry` | None |\\n| Metric prefix | Per-component namespaces (e.g., `apiserver_`, `kubelet_`) | `grafana_` namespace via `ExporterName` constant |\\n| Graphite bridge | Not built-in | Optional Graphite bridge in `InternalMetricsService.Run` |\"\n}\n",
